(******************************************************************************************

 Standard examples of enriched profunctors

 In this file, we define standard standard constructions on enriched profunctors. One of
 the constructions is given by  the identity profunctor, which is necessary to construct
 the (double) (bi)category of enriched categories. Another is given by representable
 profunctors, and those are needed to construct an equipment. Finally, we consider
 precomposition with enriched functors, and that is needed to define squares of profunctors
 in terms of enriched natural transformations.

 Contents
 1. Identity profunctor
 2. Representable profunctors
 2.1. Left representable
 2.2. Right representable
 3. Precomposition with enriched functors

 ******************************************************************************************)

(** * 1. Identity profunctor *)
Section IdentityProfunctor.
  Context {V : sym_mon_closed_cat}
          {C : category}
          (E : enrichment C V).

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
enriched_profunctor_data E E

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
enriched_profunctor_data E E

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
C → C → V
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x₁ x₂ y : C, V ⟦ (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ ?P x₁ y, ?P x₂ y ⟧
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x y₁ y₂ : C, V ⟦ (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ ?P x y₁, ?P x y₂ ⟧

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
C → C → V
 exact (λ x y, E ⦃ x , y ⦄).
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x₁ x₂ y : C,
V ⟦ (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (λ x y0 : C, E ⦃ x, y0 ⦄) x₁ y,
(λ x y0 : C, E ⦃ x, y0 ⦄) x₂ y ⟧
 exact (λ x₁ x₂ y, sym_mon_braiding V _ _ · enriched_comp _ _ _ _).
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x y₁ y₂ : C,
V ⟦ (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (λ x0 y : C, E ⦃ x0, y ⦄) x y₁,
(λ x0 y : C, E ⦃ x0, y ⦄) x y₂ ⟧
 exact (λ x y₁ y₂, enriched_comp _ _ _ _).
  Defined.

enriched_profunctor_laws
  identity_enriched_profunctor_data

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

E: enrichment C V
enriched_profunctor_laws
  identity_enriched_profunctor_data

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x y : C,
enriched_id E x
#⊗ identity (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y)
· lmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x x y =
mon_lunitor (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y)
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x y : C,
enriched_id E y
#⊗ identity (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y)
· rmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y y =
mon_lunitor (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y)
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x₁ x₂ x₃ y : C,
(sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
 · enriched_comp E x₃ x₂ x₁)
#⊗ identity (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y)
· lmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₃ y =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y)
· identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ lmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₂ y
· lmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₂ x₃ y
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x y₁ y₂ y₃ : C,
enriched_comp E y₁ y₂ y₃
#⊗ identity (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁)
· rmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁ y₃ =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁)
· identity (E ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁ y₂
· rmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₂ y₃
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ : C,
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁)
· identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ lmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₂ y₁
· rmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₂ y₁ y₂ =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁)
· identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁ y₂
· lmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₂ y₂

#⊗ identity (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y)
· lmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x x y =

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x, y: C
enriched_id E x #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x, y ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x, x ⦄) (E ⦃ x, y ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E x x y) = mon_lunitor (E ⦃ x, y ⦄)

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x, y: C
sym_mon_braiding V I_{ V} (E ⦃ x, y ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ x, y ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E x
· enriched_comp E x x y = mon_lunitor (E ⦃ x, y ⦄)

· (identity (E ⦃ x, y ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E x
   · enriched_comp E x x y) = mon_lunitor (E ⦃ x, y ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

E: enrichment C V
x, y: C
sym_mon_braiding V I_{ V} (E ⦃ x, y ⦄)
· mon_runitor (E ⦃ x, y ⦄) = mon_lunitor (E ⦃ x, y ⦄)

      apply sym_mon_braiding_runitor.

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, x₃, y: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V
     ((E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)) (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
   · (mon_rassociator (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y
        #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E x₃ x₂ y)) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E x₃ x₂ y)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, x₃, y: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V ((E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))
    (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₃ x₂ y =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₃ x₂ y

    (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄)

· sym_mon_braiding V ((E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))
    (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· (identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
   #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
   · identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
     #⊗ enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, x₃, y: C

#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V
     ((E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)) (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)
   · (mon_rassociator (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y
        #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))) =

   #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y ⦄)

      #⊗ enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y
      · sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
          (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄)))

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
∏ x y₁ y₂ y₃ : C,
enriched_comp E y₁ y₂ y₃
#⊗ identity (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁)
· rmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁ y₃ =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁)
· identity (E ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁ y₂
· rmap_e identity_enriched_profunctor_data x y₂ y₃

· enriched_comp E x y₁ y₃ =

  (E ⦃ x, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_comp E x y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E x y₂ y₃

#⊗ identity (identity_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁)

V: sym_mon_closed_cat

E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C

#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y₁)

   · enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y₂)

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y₂ =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₂ x₁ y₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₂ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· (mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
   · (identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
           (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
      · (mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
           (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
         · enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂
           #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)))) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· (identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂
   · sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₂ ⦄))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· (mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
   · (identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
           (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
      · (mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
           (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
         · enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂
           #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)))) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     ((E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄))
   · enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂
     #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    ((E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄))
· enriched_comp E x₁ y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    ((E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· (mon_rassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
     (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
   · sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
     #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
   · mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
       (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
   · identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
     #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
          (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
   · mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
       (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))

#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =

  (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄) =
identity
  ((E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄))
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E ⦃ x₁, y₁ ⦄)

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  identity_enriched_profunctor_data
 exact identity_enriched_profunctor_laws.
  Defined.

· enriched_from_arr E g #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E x₁ x₂ y) = precomp_arr E y g

   · identity (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄) #⊗ enriched_from_arr E g) =

· identity (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄) #⊗ enriched_from_arr E g =

      apply idpath.
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
y, x₁, x₂: C
g: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
mon_rinvunitor (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄)
· identity (E ⦃ x₂, y ⦄) #⊗ enriched_from_arr E g
· enriched_comp E x₁ x₂ y = precomp_arr E y g

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

E: enrichment C V

rmap_e_arr identity_enriched_profunctor f x =

    apply idpath.
  Qed.
End IdentityProfunctor.

(** * 2. Representable profunctors *)
Section Representable.
  Context {V : sym_mon_closed_cat}
          {C₁ C₂ : category}
          {F : C₁ ⟶ C₂}
          {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
          {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
          (EF : functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂).

  (** ** 2.1. Left representable *)
  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
enriched_profunctor_data E₁ E₂

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
enriched_profunctor_data E₁ E₂

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
C₂ → C₁ → V
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₂) (y : C₁),
V ⟦ (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ ?P x₁ y, ?P x₂ y ⟧
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
∏ (x : C₂) (y₁ y₂ : C₁),
V ⟦ (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ ?P x y₁, ?P x y₂ ⟧

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
C₂ → C₁ → V
 exact (λ x y, E₂ ⦃ x , F y ⦄).
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₂) (y : C₁),
V
⟦ (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  ⊗ (λ (x : C₂) (y0 : C₁), E₂ ⦃ x, F y0 ⦄) x₁ y,
(λ (x : C₂) (y0 : C₁), E₂ ⦃ x, F y0 ⦄) x₂ y ⟧
 exact (λ x₁ x₂ y, sym_mon_braiding V _ _ · enriched_comp E₂ _ _ _).
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
∏ (x : C₂) (y₁ y₂ : C₁),
V
⟦ (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  ⊗ (λ (x0 : C₂) (y : C₁), E₂ ⦃ x0, F y ⦄) x y₁,
(λ (x0 : C₂) (y : C₁), E₂ ⦃ x0, F y ⦄) x y₂ ⟧
 exact (λ x y₁ y₂, (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity _) · enriched_comp E₂ _ _ _).
  Defined.

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
enriched_profunctor_laws
  representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data

   · identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
     #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ x₃ x₂ x₁
   · enriched_comp E₂ x₃ x₁ (F y)) = ?b

        
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₂
y: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V
     ((E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))
     (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
   · (identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
      #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ x₃ x₂ x₁
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₃ x₁ (F y))) = ?b

        (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y)
        #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₃ x₂ (F y))) = ?b

        apply idpath.

EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₂
y: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V
     ((E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))
     (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
   · (mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y)
        #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₃ x₂ (F y))) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y))
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, F y ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E₂ x₃ x₂ (F y))

· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₂
y: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V ((E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)

      apply sym_mon_tensor_rassociator.
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
∏ (x : C₂) (y₁ y₂ y₃ : C₁),
enriched_comp E₁ y₁ y₂ y₃
#⊗ identity
     (representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x y₁)
· rmap_e representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x
    y₁ y₃ =
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x y₁)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e
       representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x
       y₁ y₂
· rmap_e representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x
    y₂ y₃

   · enriched_comp E₂ x (F y₁) (F y₃)) =

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂

∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₂) (y₁ y₂ : C₁),
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity
     (representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x₁
        y₁)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x₁ y₁)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ lmap_e
       representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x₁
       x₂ y₁
· rmap_e representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data
    x₂ y₁ y₂ =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x₁ y₁)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e
       representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data x₁
       y₁ y₂
· lmap_e representable_enriched_profunctor_left_data
    x₁ x₂ y₂

y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y₁))
· (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, F y₁ ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ (F y₁) (F y₂)) =

· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₁ (F y₁) (F y₂))
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₂ ⦄) · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y₂))

· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
   · identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
     #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y₁))
· (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, F y₁ ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ (F y₁) (F y₂)) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₁ (F y₁) (F y₂))
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₂ ⦄) · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y₂))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₂
y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
   · (identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
           (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
      · (identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
         #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y₁)
         · (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, F y₁ ⦄)
            · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ (F y₁) (F y₂))))) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
   #⊗ (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
       · enriched_comp E₂ x₁ (F y₁) (F y₂))
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y₂)))

y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
   · (identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
           (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
      · (EF y₁ y₂
         #⊗ identity
              ((E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))
         · (mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄)
              (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
            · enriched_comp E₂ x₁ (F y₁) (F y₂)
              #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
            · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y₂))))) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
   #⊗ (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
       · enriched_comp E₂ x₁ (F y₁) (F y₂))
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ x₂ x₁ (F y₂)))

· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)

y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· EF y₁ y₂
  #⊗ identity ((E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₂ x₁ (F y₁) (F y₂)
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    ((E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
· (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₂ x₁ (F y₁) (F y₂)
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₂
y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· EF y₁ y₂
  #⊗ identity ((E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    ((E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
· (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₂
y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
   · (identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
           (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
      · (EF y₁ y₂
         #⊗ identity
              ((E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))
         · mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄)
             (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)))) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     ((E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
   · (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
     #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂

E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₂
y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
   · (identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
           (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
      · (EF y₁ y₂
         #⊗ (identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
             #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))
         · mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄)
             (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)))) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     ((E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
   · (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
     #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))

  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =

· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)

· (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)

· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    ((E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₂
y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· (mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
     (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
   · sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
       (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
   · mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
   · identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
     #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
          (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
   · mon_rassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄))

· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

       (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) =

  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

       (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)

y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₂
y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) =
identity
  ((E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄))
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₂
y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ x₁, F y₁ ⦄)

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

C₁ → C₂ → V

E₁: enrichment C₁ V

C₁ → C₂ → V
 exact (λ x y, E₂ ⦃ F x , y ⦄).
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y : C₂),
V
⟦ (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  ⊗ (λ (x : C₁) (y0 : C₂), E₂ ⦃ F x, y0 ⦄) x₁ y,
(λ (x : C₁) (y0 : C₂), E₂ ⦃ F x, y0 ⦄) x₂ y ⟧
 exact (λ x₁ x₂ y,
             sym_mon_braiding V _ _
             · (identity _ #⊗ EF x₂ x₁)
             · enriched_comp _ _ _ _).

∏ (x : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
V
⟦ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  ⊗ (λ (x0 : C₁) (y : C₂), E₂ ⦃ F x0, y ⦄) x y₁,
(λ (x0 : C₁) (y : C₂), E₂ ⦃ F x0, y ⦄) x y₂ ⟧
 exact (λ x y₁ y₂, enriched_comp _ _ _ _).
  Defined.

   · enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F x) y) =

   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
      · (identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) #⊗ EF x₃ x₁
         · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₃) (F x₁) y))) = ?b

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y: C₂
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V
     ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))
     (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
   · (identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
      #⊗ (EF x₂ x₁ #⊗ EF x₃ x₂)
      · (mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
           (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₃, F x₂ ⦄)
         · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) (F x₁) y
           #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₃, F x₂ ⦄)
         · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₃) (F x₂) y))) =
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
      · identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) #⊗ EF x₂ x₁
      · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) (F x₁) y)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, y ⦄)
   · identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, y ⦄) #⊗ EF x₃ x₂
   · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₃) (F x₂) y)

           (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₃, F x₂ ⦄)
         · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) (F x₁) y
           #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₃, F x₂ ⦄))))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

  (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
   #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
         (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
       · (identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) #⊗ EF x₂ x₁
          · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) (F x₁) y))
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, y ⦄)
      · identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, y ⦄) #⊗ EF x₃ x₂)) =

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y: C₂
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
     ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄))
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
      · ((identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) #⊗ EF x₂ x₁)
         #⊗ EF x₃ x₂
         · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) (F x₁) y
           #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₃, F x₂ ⦄)))) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V
     ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))
     (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
   · (identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
      #⊗ (EF x₂ x₁ #⊗ EF x₃ x₂)
      · (mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
           (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₃, F x₂ ⦄)
         · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) (F x₁) y
           #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₃, F x₂ ⦄))))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂

y: C₂
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
    ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄))
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
· (identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) #⊗ EF x₂ x₁) #⊗ EF x₃ x₂
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) (F x₁) y
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₃, F x₂ ⦄) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V
    ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) #⊗ (EF x₂ x₁ #⊗ EF x₃ x₂)
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄)

  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₃, F x₂ ⦄)

    ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y: C₂
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
    (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V
    ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄))
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)

identity
  ((E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
   ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y ⦄))

· (sym_mon_braiding V

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
∏ (x : C₁) (y₁ y₂ y₃ : C₂),
enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
#⊗ identity
     (representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data x
        y₁)
· rmap_e representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data
    x y₁ y₃ =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data x y₁)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e
       representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data x
       y₁ y₂
· rmap_e representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data
    x y₂ y₃
 
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

x: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x, y₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x) y₁ y₃ =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ F x, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ (F x) y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x) y₂ y₃

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity
     (representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data x₁
        y₁)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data x₁
       y₁)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ lmap_e
       representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data x₁
       x₂ y₁
· rmap_e representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data
    x₂ y₁ y₂ =
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data x₁ y₁)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e
       representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data x₁
       y₁ y₂
· lmap_e representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data
    x₁ x₂ y₂
 
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
      · identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄) #⊗ EF x₂ x₁
      · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) (F x₁) y₁)
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) y₁ y₂ =
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ (F x₁) y₁ y₂
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ EF x₂ x₁
   · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₂) (F x₁) y₂)

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
     ((E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄))
   · (identity ((E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄))
      #⊗ EF x₂ x₁
      · enriched_comp E₂ (F x₁) y₁ y₂
        #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄))) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
      · identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄) #⊗ EF x₂ x₁)
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x₁) y₁ y₂
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    ((E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄))
· identity ((E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄))
  #⊗ EF x₂ x₁
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x₁) y₁ y₂
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
      · identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄) #⊗ EF x₂ x₁)
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x₁) y₁ y₂
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₂, F x₁ ⦄)

  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂ ⦃ F x₁, y₁ ⦄)

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
enriched_profunctor E₂ E₁

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
enriched_profunctor E₂ E₁

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
enriched_profunctor_data E₂ E₁
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
enriched_profunctor_laws ?P

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
enriched_profunctor_data E₂ E₁
 exact representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data.
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
enriched_profunctor_laws
  representable_enriched_profunctor_right_data
 exact representable_enriched_profunctor_right_laws.
  Defined.
End Representable.

(** * 3. Precomposition with enriched functors *)
Section Precomposition.
  Context {V : sym_mon_closed_cat}
          {C₁ C₂ C₁' C₂' : category}
          {F : C₁ ⟶ C₁'}
          {G : C₂ ⟶ C₂'}
          {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
          {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
          {E₁' : enrichment C₁' V}
          {E₂' : enrichment C₂' V}
          (EF : functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁')
          (EG : functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂')
          (P : E₁' ↛e E₂').

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'
G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
enriched_profunctor_data E₁ E₂

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'
G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
enriched_profunctor_data E₁ E₂

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'
G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
C₂ → C₁ → V
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'
G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'
E₁: enrichment C₁ V

E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₂) (y : C₁),
V ⟦ (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) ⊗ ?P x₁ y, ?P x₂ y ⟧
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'
G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
∏ (x : C₂) (y₁ y₂ : C₁),
V ⟦ (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ ?P x y₁, ?P x y₂ ⟧

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'
G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
C₂ → C₁ → V
 exact (λ x y, P (G x) (F y)).
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'
G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₂) (y : C₁),
V
⟦ (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  ⊗ (λ (x : C₂) (y0 : C₁), P (G x) (F y0)) x₁ y,
(λ (x : C₂) (y0 : C₁), P (G x) (F y0)) x₂ y ⟧
 exact (λ x₁ x₂ y,
             (EG x₂ x₁ #⊗ identity _) · lmap_e P (G x₁) (G x₂) (F y)).
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'
G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
∏ (x : C₂) (y₁ y₂ : C₁),
V
⟦ (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  ⊗ (λ (x0 : C₂) (y : C₁), P (G x0) (F y)) x y₁,
(λ (x0 : C₂) (y : C₁), P (G x0) (F y)) x y₂ ⟧
 exact (λ x y₁ y₂,
             (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity _) · rmap_e P (G x) (F y₁) (F y₂)).
  Defined.

#⊗ identity (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y)
· lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x x y =
mon_lunitor (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y)

enriched_id E₁ y
#⊗ identity (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y)
· rmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y y =
mon_lunitor (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y)
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'

∏ (x₁ x₂ x₃ : C₂) (y : C₁),
(sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
 · enriched_comp E₂ x₃ x₂ x₁)
#⊗ identity (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y)
· lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₃ y =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₂ y
· lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₂ x₃ y
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

· rmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁ y₃ =

  (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁ y₂
· rmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y₂ y₃

· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁ y₂
· lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₂ y₂

      apply idpath.

      apply idpath.

EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
∏ (x₁ x₂ x₃ : C₂) (y : C₁),
(sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
 · enriched_comp E₂ x₃ x₂ x₁)
#⊗ identity (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y)
· lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₃ y =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₂ y
· lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₂ x₃ y

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category

y: C₁
?b =
(sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₃, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
 · EG x₂ x₁ #⊗ EG x₃ x₂) #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y))
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
    (E₂' ⦃ G x₃, G x₂ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y))
· mon_lassociator (E₂' ⦃ G x₃, G x₂ ⦄)
    (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄) (P (G x₁) (F y))
· identity (E₂' ⦃ G x₃, G x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ lmap_e P (G x₁) (G x₂) (F y)

∏ (x : C₂) (y₁ y₂ y₃ : C₁),
enriched_comp E₁ y₁ y₂ y₃
#⊗ identity (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x y₁)

sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁)
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₂ y₁
· rmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₂ y₁ y₂ =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ y₁ y₂
· lmap_e precomp_enriched_profunctor_data x₁ x₂ y₂
 
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'

E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V

EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
x₁, x₂: C₂
y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (EG x₂ x₁ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
      · lmap_e P (G x₁) (G x₂) (F y₁))
· (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (P (G x₂) (F y₁))
   · rmap_e P (G x₂) (F y₁) (F y₂)) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
      · rmap_e P (G x₁) (F y₁) (F y₂))
· (EG x₂ x₁ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₂))
   · lmap_e P (G x₁) (G x₂) (F y₂))

                (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
              #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))

            · lmap_e P (G x₁) (G x₂) (F y₂))))) =

· identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ (EG x₂ x₁ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁)))
· EF y₁ y₂
  #⊗ identity ((E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄) ⊗ P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· mon_rassociator (E₁' ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄)
    (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄) (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₁' ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄)
    (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· mon_lassociator (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
    (E₁' ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄) (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· identity (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e P (G x₁) (F y₁) (F y₂) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
      · rmap_e P (G x₁) (F y₁) (F y₂))
· EG x₂ x₁ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₂))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

#⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
    (P (G x₁) (F y₁))

  #⊗ identity ((E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄) ⊗ P (G x₁) (F y₁))

· identity (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)

y₁, y₂: C₁
(EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ EG x₂ x₁) #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁' ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄)
     (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
   #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
   · (mon_lassociator (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
        (E₁' ⦃ F y₁, F y₂ ⦄) (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
      · identity (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
        #⊗ rmap_e P (G x₁) (F y₁) (F y₂))) = ?t2

E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
x₁, x₂: C₂
y₁, y₂: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
#⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
   #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
   · mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
       (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
   · EG x₂ x₁
     #⊗ (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁)))
   · identity (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
     #⊗ rmap_e P (G x₁) (F y₁) (F y₂)) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
      · rmap_e P (G x₁) (F y₁) (F y₂))
· EG x₂ x₁ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₂))

· identity (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e P (G x₁) (F y₁) (F y₂) =
mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  (P (G x₁) (F y₁))
· EG x₂ x₁ #⊗ (EF y₁ y₂ #⊗ identity (P (G x₁) (F y₁)))
· identity (E₂' ⦃ G x₂, G x₁ ⦄)
  #⊗ rmap_e P (G x₁) (F y₁) (F y₂)

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C₁, C₂, C₁', C₂': category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₁'
G: C₂ ⟶ C₂'
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₁': enrichment C₁' V
E₂': enrichment C₂' V
EF: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₁'
EG: functor_enrichment G E₂ E₂'
P: enriched_profunctor E₁' E₂'
enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
